<s> GREX OF MONTE CARLO CHAPTER I AN UNEXPECTED MEETING The eyes of the man who had looked in upon a scene inordinately, fantastically brilliant, underwent, after those first few moments of comparative indifference, a curious transformation </s>
<s> He was contemplating one of the sights of the world </s>
<s> Crowded around the two roulette tables, promenading or lounging on the heavily cushioned divans against the wall, he took note of a conglomeration of people representing, perhaps, every grade of society, every nationality of importance, yet with a curious common likeness by reason of their tribute paid to fashion </s>
<s> He glanced unmoved at a beautiful Englishwoman who was a duchess but looked otherwise; at an equally beautiful Frenchwoman, who looked like a duchess but was--otherwise </s>
<s> On every side of him were women gowned by the great artists of the day, women like flowers, all perfume and softness and colour </s>
<s> His eyes passed them over almost carelessly </s>
<s> A little tired with many weeks' travel in countries where the luxuries of life were few, his senses were dulled to the magnificence of the scene, his pulses as yet had not responded to its charm and wonder </s>
<s> And then the change came </s>
<s> He saw a woman standing almost exactly opposite to him at the nearest roulette table, and he gave a noticeable start </s>
<s> For a moment his pale, expressionless face was transformed, his secret was at any one's mercy </s>
<s> That, however, was the affair of an instant only </s>
<s> He was used to shocks and he survived this one </s>
<s> He moved a little on one side from his prominent place in the centre of the wide-flung doorway </s>
<s> He stood by one of the divans and watched </s>
<s> She was tall and fair and slight </s>
<s> She wore a high-necked gown of shimmering grey, a black hat, under which her many coils of hair shone like gold, and a necklace of pearls around her throat, pearls on which his eyes had rested with a curious expression </s>
<s> She played, unlike many of her neighbours, with restraint, yet with interest, almost enthusiasm </s>
<s> There was none of the strain of the gambler about her smooth, beautiful face </s>
<s> Her delicately curved lips were free from the grim lines of concentrated acquisitiveness </s>
<s> She was thirty-two years old but she looked much younger as she stood there, her lips a little parted in a pleased smile of anticipation </s>
<s> She was leaning a little over the table and her eyes were fixed with humorous intentness upon the spinning wheel </s>
<s> Even amongst that crowd of beautiful women she possessed a certain individual distinction </s>
<s> She not only looked what she was--an Englishwoman of good birth--but there was a certain delicate aloofness about her expression and bearing which gave an added charm to a personality which seemed to combine the two extremes of provocativeness and reserve </s>
<s> One would have hesitated to address to her even the chance remarks which pass so easily between strangers around the tables </s>
<s> "Violet here" </s>
<s> the man murmured under his breath </s>
<s> "Violet" </s>
<s> There was tragedy in the whisper, a gleam of something like tragedy, too, in the look which passed between the man and the woman a few moments later </s>
<s> With her hands full of plaques which she had just won, she raised her eyes at last from the board </s>
<s> The smile upon her lips was the delighted smile of a girl </s>
<s> And then, as she was in the act of sweeping her winnings into her gold bag, she saw the man opposite </s>
<s> The smile seemed to die from her lips; it appeared, indeed, to pass with all else of expression from her face </s>
<s> The plaques dropped one by one through her fingers, into the satchel </s>
<s> Her eyes remained fixed upon him as though she were looking upon a ghost </s>
<s> The seconds seemed drawn out into a grim hiatus of time </s>
<s> The croupier's voice, the muttered imprecation of a loser by her side, the necessity of making some slight movement in order to allow the passage of an arm from some one in search of change--some such trifle at last brought her back from the shadows </s>
<s> Her expression became at once more normal </s>
<s> She did not remove her eyes but she very slightly inclined her head towards the man </s>
<s> He, in return, bowed very gravely and without a smile </s>
<s> The table in front of her was cleared now </s>
<s> People were beginning to consider their next coup </s>
<s> The voice of the croupier, with his parrot-like cry, travelled down the board </s>
<s> _"Faites vos jeux, mesdames et messieurs"._ The woman made no effort to stake </s>
<s> After a moment's hesitation she yielded up her place, and moving backwards, seated herself upon an empty divan </s>
<s> Rapidly the thoughts began to form themselves in her mind </s>
<s> Her delicate eyebrows drew closer together in a distinct frown </s>
<s> After that first shock, that queer turmoil of feeling, beyond analysis, yet having within it some entirely unexpected constituent, she found herself disposed to be angry </s>
<s> The sensation had not subsided when a moment or two later she was conscious that the man whose coming had proved so disturbing was standing before her </s>
<s> "Good afternoon," he said, a little stiffly </s>
<s> She raised her eyes </s>
<s> The frown was still upon her forehead, although to a certain extent it was contradicted by a slight tremulousness of the lips </s>
<s> "Good afternoon, Henry" </s>
<s> For some reason or other, further speech seemed to him a difficult matter </s>
<s> He moved towards the vacant place </s>
<s> "If you have no objection," he observed, as he seated himself </s>
<s> She unfurled her fan--an ancient but wonderful weapon of defence </s>
<s> It gave her a brief respite </s>
<s> Then she looked at him calmly </s>
<s> "Of all places in the world," she murmured, "to meet you here" </s>
<s> "Is it so extraordinary" </s>
<s> "I find it so," she admitted </s>
<s> "You don't at all fit in, you know </s>
<s> A scene like this," she added, glancing around, "would scarcely ever be likely to attract you for its own sake, would it" </s>
<s> "It doesn't particularly," he admitted </s>
<s> "Then why have you come" </s>
<s> He remained silent </s>
<s> The frown upon her forehead deepened </s>
<s> "Perhaps," she went on coldly, "I can help you with your reply </s>
<s> You have come because you are not satisfied with the reports of the private detective whom you have engaged to watch me </s>
<s> You have come to supplement them by your own investigation" </s>
<s> His frown matched hers </s>
<s> The coldness of his tone was rendered even more bitter by its note of anger </s>
<s> "I am surprised that you should have thought me capable of such an action," he declared </s>
<s> "All I can say is that it is thoroughly in keeping with your other suspicions of me, and that I find it absolutely unworthy" </s>
<s> She laughed a little incredulously, not altogether naturally </s>
<s> "My dear Henry," she protested, "I cannot flatter myself that there is any other person in the world sufficiently interested in my movements to have me watched" </s>
<s> "Are you really under the impression that that is the case" </s>
<s> he enquired grimly </s>
<s> "It isn't a matter of impression at all," she retorted </s>
<s> "It is the truth </s>
<s> I was followed from London, I was watched at Cannes, I am watched here day by day--by a little man in a brown suit and a Homburg hat, and with a habit of lounging </s>
<s> He lounges under my windows, he is probably lounging across the way now </s>
<s> He has lounged within fifty yards of me for the last three weeks, and to tell you the truth I am tired of him </s>
<s> Couldn't I have a week's holiday </s>

<s> She turned and looked at him </s>
<s> His tone was convincing </s>
<s> He had not the face of a man whose word of honour was a negligible thing </s>
<s> "But, Henry," she protested, "I tell you that there is no doubt about the matter </s>
<s> I am watched day and night--I, an insignificant person whose doings can be of no possible interest save to you and you only" </s>
<s> The man did not at once reply </s>
<s> His thoughts seemed to have wandered off for a moment </s>
<s> When he spoke again, his tone had lost its note of resentment </s>
<s> "I do not blame you for your suspicion," he said calmly, "although I can assure you that I have never had any idea of having you watched </s>

<s> She was puzzled--at once puzzled and interested </s>
<s> "I am so glad to hear this," she said, "and of course I believe you, but there the fact is </s>
<s> I think that you will agree with me that it is curious" </s>
<s> "Isn't it possible," he ventured to suggest, "that it is your companions who are the object of this man's vigilance </s>
<s> You are not, I presume, alone here" </s>
<s> She eyed him a little defiantly </s>
<s> "I am here," she announced, "with Mr and Mrs Draconmeyer" </s>

<s> "Certainly </s>

<s> CHAPTER III A WARNING Hunterleys dined alone at a small round table, set in a remote corner of the great restaurant attached to the Hotel de Paris </s>
<s> The scene around him was full of colour and interest </s>
<s> A scarlet-coated band made wonderful music </s>
<s> The toilettes of the women who kept passing backwards and forwards, on their way to the various tables, were marvellous; in their way unique </s>
<s> The lights and flowers of the room, its appointments and adornments, all represented the last word in luxury </s>
<s> Everywhere was colour, everywhere an almost strained attempt to impress upon the passerby the fact that this was no ordinary holiday resort but the giant pleasure-ground of all in the world who had money to throw away and the capacity for enjoyment </s>
<s> Only once a more somber note seemed struck when Mrs Draconmeyer, leaning on her husband's arm and accompanied by a nurse and Lady Hunterleys, passed to their table </s>
<s> Hunterleys' eyes followed the little party until they had reached their destination and taken their places </s>
<s> His wife was wearing black and she had discarded the pearls which had hung around her neck during the afternoon </s>
<s> She wore only a collar of diamonds, his gift </s>
<s> Her hair was far less elaborately coiffured and her toilette less magnificent than the toilettes of the women by whom she was surrounded </s>

<s> There was no other woman in the whole of that great restaurant with her air of quiet elegance; no other woman so faultless in the smaller details of her toilette and person </s>

<s> It was a cursed mischance which had brought him to Monte Carlo </s>

<s> CHAPTER XIII MISS GREX AT HOME Richard Lane, as he made his way up the avenue towards the Villa Mimosa, wondered whether he was not indeed finding his way into fairyland </s>
<s> On either side of him were drooping mimosa trees, heavy with the snaky, orange-coloured blossom whose perfumes hung heavy upon the windless air </s>

<s> The front-door was wide open, and before he could reach the bell a butler had appeared </s>
<s> "Is Mr Grex at home" </s>

<s> CHAPTER XV INTERNATIONAL POLITICS The Villa Mimosa flamed with lights from the top story to the ground-floor </s>
<s> The entrance gates stood wide-open </s>

<s> CHAPTER XVII DUTY INTERFERES AGAIN Hunterleys sat that night alone in a seat at the Opera for a time and lost himself in a maze of recollections </s>
<s> He seemed to find himself growing younger as he listened to the music </s>
<s> The days of a more vivid and ardent sentimentality seemed to reassert themselves </s>

<s> CHAPTER XX WILY MR </s>
<s> DRACONMEYER They had skirted the wonderful bay and climbed the mountainous hill to the frontier before Violet spoke </s>
<s> All the time Draconmeyer leaned back by her side, perfectly content </s>
<s> A man of varied subtleties, he understood and fully appreciated the intrinsic value of silence </s>

<s> CHAPTER XXI ASSASSINATION </s>
<s> Selingman, a large cigar between his lips and a happy smile upon his face, stood in the square before the Casino, watching the pigeons </s>
<s> He had just enjoyed an excellent lunch, he was exceedingly pleased with a new light grey suit which he was wearing, and his one unsatisfied desire was for companionship </s>
<s> Draconmeyer was away motoring with Lady Hunterleys, Mr Grex was spending the early part of the day in conclave with their visitor from France, and Mademoiselle Nipon had gone to Nice for the day </s>
<s> Selingman had been left to his own devices and was beginning to find time hang upon his hands </s>
<s> Conversation and companionship were almost as great necessities with him as wine </s>
<s> He beamed upon the pigeons and looked around at the people dotted about in chairs outside the Café de Paris, hoping to find an acquaintance </s>
<s> It chanced, however, that he saw nothing but strangers </s>
<s> Then his eyes fell upon a man who was seated with folded arms a short distance away, a man of respectable but somewhat gloomy appearance, dressed in dark clothes, with pale cheeks and cavernous eyes </s>
<s> Selingman strolled towards him </s>
<s> "How go things, friend Allen" </s>
<s> he enquired, dropping his voice a little </s>
<s> The man glanced uneasily around </s>
<s> There was, however, no one in his immediate vicinity </s>
<s> "Badly," he admitted </s>
<s> "Still no success, eh" </s>
<s> Selingman asked, drawing up a chair and seating himself </s>
<s> "The man is secretive by nature," was the gloomy reply </s>
<s> "One would imagine that he knew he was being watched </s>
<s> Everything which he receives in the way of a written communication is at once torn up </s>
<s> He is the most difficult order of person to deal with--he is methodical </s>
<s> He has only the hotel valet to look after his things but everything is always in its place </s>
<s> Yesterday I went through his waste-paper basket </s>
<s> I took home the contents but the pieces were no larger than sixpences </s>
<s> I was able to put together one envelope which he received yesterday morning, which was franked 'On His Majesty's Service,' and the post-mark of which was Downing Street" </s>
<s> Selingman shook his head ponderously and then replied seriously: "You must do better than that, my Sherlock Holmes--much better" </s>
<s> "I can't make bricks without straw," Allen retorted sullenly </s>
<s> "There is always straw if one looks in the right place," Selingman insisted, puffing away at his cigar </s>
<s> "What we want to discover is, exactly how much does Hunterleys know of certain operations of ours which are going on here </s>
<s> He is on the watch--that I am sure of </s>
<s> There is one known agent in the place, and another suspected one, and I am pretty certain that they are both working at his instigation </s>
<s> What we want to get hold of is one of his letters to London" </s>
<s> "I have been in and out of his rooms at all hours," the other said </s>
<s> "I have gone into the matter thoroughly, so thoroughly that I have taken a situation with a firm of English tailors here, and I am supposed to go out and tout for orders </s>
<s> That gives me a free entrée to the hotel </s>
<s> I have even had a commission from Sir Henry himself </s>
<s> He gave me a coat to get some buttons sewn on </s>
<s> I am practically free of his room but what's the good </s>
<s> He doesn't even lead the Monte Carlo life </s>
<s> He doesn't give one a chance of getting at him through a third person </s>
<s> No notes from ladies, no flower or jewelry bills, not the shadow of an assignation </s>
<s> The only photograph upon his table is a photograph of Lady Hunterleys" </s>
<s> "Better not tell our friend Draconmeyer that," Selingman observed, smiling to himself </s>
<s> "Well, well, you can do nothing but persevere, Allen </s>
<s> We are not niggardly masters </s>
<s> If a man fails through no fault of his own, well, we don't throw him into the street </s>
<s> Nothing parsimonious about us </s>
<s> No need for you to sit about with a face as long as a fiddle because you can't succeed all at once </s>
<s> We are the people to kick at it, not you </s>
<s> Drink a little more wine, my friend </s>
<s> Give yourself a liqueur after luncheon </s>
<s> Stick a cigar in your mouth and go and sit in the sunshine </s>
<s> Make friends with some of the ladies </s>
<s> Remember, the sun will still shine and the music play in fifty years' time, but not for you </s>
<s> Come and see me when you want some more money" </s>
<s> "You are very kind, sir," the man replied </s>
<s> "I am going across to the hotel now </s>
<s> Sir Henry has been about there most of the morning but he has just gone in to Ciro's to lunch, so I shall have at least half-an-hour" </s>
<s> "Good luck to you" </s>
<s> Selingman exclaimed heartily </s>

<s> I am hopeful for you this afternoon, Allen </s>
<s> I believe you are going to do well </s>

<s> Selingman climbed the hill and entered the hotel where he was staying </s>
<s> He mounted to his room, took off his coat, at which he glanced admiringly for a moment and then hung up behind the door </s>
<s> Finally he pulled down the blinds and lay down to rest </s>
<s> Very soon he was asleep... </s>
<s> The drowsy afternoon wore on </s>
<s> Through the open windows came the sound of carriages driven along the dusty way, the shouts of the coachmen to their horses, the jingling of bells, the hooting of motor horns </s>

<s> CHAPTER XXXVII AN AMAZING ELOPEMENT The sun was shining brilliantly and the sky was cloudless as Richard turned his automobile into the grounds of the Villa Mimosa, soon after nine o'clock on the following morning </s>
<s> The yellow-blossomed trees, slightly stirred by the west wind, formed a golden arch across the winding avenue </s>

<s> "What would you like to do afterwards" </s>
<s> he asked </s>
<s> "I think," she replied, leaning towards him, "that I should like to go to that nice Englishman who lets villas, and find one right at the edge of the sea, quite hidden, and lock the gates, and give no one our address, and have you forget for just one month that there was any work to do in the world, or any one else in it except me" </s>
<s> "Just to make up," he laughed softly </s>
<s> "Women are like that, you know," she murmured </s>
<s> "The man's office is this way," Hunterleys said, turning off the main street </s>
<s> THE END * * * * * E </s>
